***сыпать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:сыпать.html>сы́пать</a> (8437)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">сꙑпати</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sypati</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*sỳpati</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to pour, strew</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сыпать.html>сы́пать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sýpatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:насыпать.html>насы́пать</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:посыпать.html>посы́пать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">also figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to pour <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of friable/solid objects, such as sand; not liquids</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:сыпать.html>сы́пать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:острота.html>остро́тами</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>sýpatʹ</b> ostrótami</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to witticize</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:сыпать.html>сы́пать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:соль.html>соль</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:рана.html>ра́ну</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>sýpatʹ</b> solʹ na ránu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to pour salt on the wound, to rub it in</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to squander
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:сыпать.html>сы́пать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:деньги.html>де́ньгами</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>sýpatʹ</b> dénʹgami</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to squander money</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<div class="derivedterms" style="column-count: 2; -moz-column-count: 2; -ms-column-count: 2; -o-column-count: 2; -webkit-column-count: 2;;">
<p><i>imperfective</i>
</p>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сыпаться.html>сы́паться</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">sýpatʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сыпать.html>сыпа́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">sypátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

***сыпаться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:сыпаться.html>сы́паться</a> (6128)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сыпать.html>сы́пать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sýpatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сыпаться.html>сы́паться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sýpatʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">насы́паться</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:посыпаться.html>посы́паться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to fall, to pour, to run out
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:штукатурка.html>штукату́рка</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:сыпаться.html>сы́плется</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">štukatúrka <b>sýpletsja</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">the plaster flakes off</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to rain down, to pour forth
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:сыпаться.html>сы́паться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:град.html>гра́дом</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>sýpatʹsja</b> grádom</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to hail <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">precipitation</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>, <span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to rain down</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to fall thick and fast
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:удар.html>уда́ры</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:сыпаться.html>сыпа́лись</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:град.html>гра́дом</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">udáry <b>sypálisʹ</b> grádom</i> ― <span class="e-translation">blows were raining down (falling thick and fast)</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <i>(of cloth)</i> to fray out</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to flunk, to fail</li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сыпать.html>сы́пать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sýpatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

***сыпучий.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:сыпучий.html>сыпу́чий</a> (19901)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сыпать.html>сы́пать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sýpatʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to pour (of friable/solid objects)</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-у́чий</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-účij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сыпучий.html>сыпу́чий</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sypúčij</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)<a href = vnd.unilang:сыпучий.html>сыпу́чее</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)<a href = vnd.unilang:сыпучий.html>сыпу́чей</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>loose, friable, free-flowing</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:сырой.html>сыр</a> (5018)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_5">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*syrъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">cheese</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Balto-Slavic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Balto-Slavic language">Proto-Balto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-bsl-pro">*sū́ˀras</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*SuHrós</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_6">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***сырой.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:сырой.html>сыро́й</a> (2376)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*syrъ</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*SúHros</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">sour, salty, bitter</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, whence English <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">sour</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сырой.html>сыро́й</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">syrój</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)сыре́е</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)<a href = vnd.unilang:сырье.html>сыре́й</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>damp, moist</li>
<li>raw, uncooked, unbaked</li>
<li>crude</li>
<li>green, unripe</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:влажный.html>вла́жный</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">vlážnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

***сырок.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:сырок.html>сыро́к</a> (27667)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сырой.html>сыр</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">syr</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-о́к</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ók</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:сытный.html>сы́тный</a> (16570)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сытый.html>сы́т</a>(ый)</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sýt(yj)</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сытный.html>сы́тный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sýtnyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)сытне́е</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)сытне́й</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>hearty, filling <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">meal, food</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li>having plenty of food
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:сытный.html>сы́тное</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:время.html>вре́мя</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>sýtnoje</b> vrémja</i> ― <span class="e-translation">time of <b>plenty</b></span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial<span class="ib-comma">,</span> figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> prosperous</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial<span class="ib-comma">,</span> figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> lucrative</li></ol>

***сытый.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:сытый.html>сы́тый</a> (4842)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*sytъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">satiated, full</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*s(e)h₂tos</i>, from <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*seh₂-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to satiate</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сытый.html>сы́тый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sýtyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)сыте́е</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)сыте́й</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>satiated</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> satisfied, full, sated</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сыч.html>сыч</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">syč</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сыч.html>сыча́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сыч.html>сычи́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сыч.html>сыче́й</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>an owl of genus <i>Athene</i> or <i>Aegolius</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:домовый.html>домо́вый</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:сыч.html>сыч</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">domóvyj <b>syč</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">(<i>Athene noctua</i>) little owl</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">мохноно́гий <b><a href = vnd.unilang:сыч.html>сыч</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">moxnonógij <b>syč</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">(<i>Aegolius funereus</i>) boreal owl</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">poetic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> owl (any bird of the order <i>Strigiformes</i>)</li>
<li>reclusive person</li></ol>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сыщик.html>сы́щик</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sýščik</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сыщик.html>сы́щика</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сыщик.html>сы́щики</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сыщик.html>сы́щиков</a></b>, <i>feminine</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">сы́щица</b>)

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:сэкономить.html>сэконо́мить</a> (11718)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">с-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">s-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:экономить.html>эконо́мить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ekonómitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сэкономить.html>сэконо́мить</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sɛkonómitʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:экономить.html>эконо́мить</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to save
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:сэкономить.html>сэконо́мить</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:время.html>вре́мя</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>sɛkonómitʹ</b> vrémja</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to save time</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:сэкономить.html>сэконо́мить</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> чём-либо</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>sɛkonómitʹ</b> na čóm-libo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to save on something, to spend less on something</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
